　　腰痛方　腰痛脉大者，肾虚也，宜此。　　杜仲　龟板　黄蘗　知母　枸杞五味各等分　　右为末，猪脊髓为丸。
　　又方　治五般腰痛。
　　胡桃肉五个，去皮研为膏　五灵脂　萆薢炒　黑牵牛炒　白牵牛炒，各三钱　狗脊半两，微炒　没药三十文　巴豆五粒，用湿纸裹煨，取肉去油　　右件为末，将前胡桃膏和入，酢糊丸，如桐子大，每服十五丸。风腰疼，豆淋无灰酒下；气腰疼，煨葱白酒下；血腰痛，当归酒下；打扑腰疼，苏木酒下。
　　防风汤　治伤寒腰痛，或皮肉(疒帬)痹，腿膝疼痛，行步艰难，不可俯仰。　　防风　芎藭　附子炮，去皮脐　当归　芍药　羌活　续断各一两　麻黄去节　桂枝去皮　杜仲炙，各七钱半　牛膝　五加皮　丹参各半两　　右(口父)咀，每服五钱，水一盏半，姜二钱同煎，食前服。[64p]

Treatment for Lower Back Pain

For lower back pain with a strong pulse, it indicates kidney deficiency; this prescription is suitable.

Ingredients:

  • Eucommia
  • Turtle shell
  • Yellow berberine
  • Anemarrhena
  • Goji berries

All equal portions, grind into a powder, and form into pills with pig spinal marrow.

Another prescription for various kinds of lower back pain:

  • Five pieces of walnut meat, skin removed and ground into a paste
  • Five Lingzhi (mushroom)
  • Processed Acorus tatarinowii
  • Fried black morning glory
  • Fried white morning glory, each three qian
  • Half a liang of dog spine, lightly fried
  • Thirty wen of myrrh
  • Five pieces of colocasia bean, wrapped in wet paper and steamed to extract meat and oil

Grind the above into a powder, mix with the walnut paste, and form into pills the size of a tung seed, taking fifteen pills each time. For different types of pain:

  • Wind-related back pain, take with warm liquor without ash
  • Qi-related back pain, take with cooked green onion liquor
  • Blood-related back pain, take with Angelica liquor
  • Pain from strikes, take with sandalwood liquor.

Jiawei Siwu Decoction: Treats lumbar pain from blood stasis. Ingredients: raw Rehmannia, Dong Quai, Chuanxiong, Peony, peach kernel paste, safflower with wine. Boil all six ingredients together and take hot on an empty stomach.

Yishen Pill: Also known as Stewed Kidney Powder, treats lumbar pain from strains and water retention causing pain. Ingredients: powdered Gansui (3 qian), pig kidney, salted and spiced to remove water, mix in medicine (3 qian) and pack inside a lotus leaf, cook over medium and slow fire until done. Chew well and take with wine.

Qianghuo and Peach Kernel Decoction: Treats falls and strains with energy and blood stagnation resulting in effective relief of lumbar pain. Ingredients: Qianghuo, peach kernel paste, safflower, cowbane washed in wine, Yanhusuo, and rhubarb with wine, equal parts. Finely chop together, taking 5 qian at a time, boil in 2 cups of water with one green onion until reduced to one cup, and take before meals.

Nian Tong Decoction: Treats damp-heat diseases causing heavy shoulders and back, limb joints, and waist pain, as well as chest discomfort. Ingredients: Bai Zhu (1.5 qian), Ginseng, Shengma, bitter Kuthan pan-fried with wine, Kudzu root, and Cang Zhu (2.5 qian), Fangfeng without roots, Zhimu without hair, both washed in wine, Ze Xie, Huang Qin, and Zhu Ling with skin removed, Dong Quai (2 qian), raw Huang Qin washed in wine, roasted Licorice, Yin Chen pan-fried with wine, Qianghuo (2.5 qian). Finely chop, combine, and boil in 2 cups of water until reduced to 1 cup, strain and take warm.[65p]

　　苍朮复煎散　治寒湿相合，脑后痛，恶寒，项筋脊骨强，肩背膝眼病，腰痛，膝膑痛，无力，行步沉重。　　红花一分　黄蘗三分　柴胡　槁本　泽泻　白朮　升麻各五分　羌活一钱　苍朮四两　　右细切，先以苍朮一味，用水三大盏，煎至二盏，去滓，入前药复煎至一盏，去滓，空心稍热服，取微汗为效。忌酒及欲。

Cang Zhu Decoction: This is used to treat the combination of cold and dampness, symptoms include pain at the back of the head, aversion to cold, stiffness in the neck, spine and bones, shoulder, back, eye, and knee pain, lumbar pain, knee joint weakness, and a feeling of heaviness when walking.

Ingredients:

  • 1 part red flower
  • 3 parts Huangbo
  • 5 parts Chaihu, Gaoben, Zexie, Baizhu, and Shengma
  • 1 qian Qianghuo
  • 4 liang Cangzhu

Preparation: Cut finely, use the Cangzhu alone first with three large cups of water, boil down to two cups, strain, then add the previously mentioned ingredients and boil down to one cup, strain again. Take on an empty stomach slightly warm, resulting in mild sweating. Avoid alcohol and desire.

Zhuo Hu Dan treats pain from stagnant blood.

  • White resin, divided into halves
  • Aconite
  • Five-spice resin
  • Hu Lu Zi, shell removed
  • Di Long, cleaned of dirt, each one tael
  • Musk
  • Beijing ink, each two and a half coins
  • Frankincense
  • Myrrh
  • Angelica, each seven and a half coins
    Mix into a fine powder, make into pills the size of tung seeds, each dose being one to two pills, up to three to five pills, taken with warm wine on an empty stomach. Note that white resin refers to the resin of the sweetgum tree; this is not sold in pharmacies—what is commonly available is white pine resin, which is not the original intent. If needed, it should be collected in summer from sweetgum trees in the mountains for optimal effect.

Zhu Fu Decoction
[From "Remarkable and Effective Formulas"]
For treating dampness injuring the kidney channel, with symptoms of heavy and cold pain in the lower back and frequent urination.

Aconite Powder
For treating lumbar pain with stiffness, unable to bend or look up, and with tightness in the muscles and tendons.
Prepare Aconite, processed; Angelica, chopped and stir-fried, each 1 liang; Eucommia bark peeled and stir-fried to remove fibers; Corydalis; Qianghuo, each 1 liang; Fangfeng, 2 liang; Cinnamon heart, 0.5 liang; Niuxi, 0.3 liang.
Grind these well. For each dose, take 4 qian, mix with 1 medium cup of water, add 0.5 qian of fresh ginger, and decoct down to 6 fen. Strain and take warm before meals.

Niuxi Pill
For treating pain in the lower back and hips, with discomfort in the limbs, unable to eat or drink.
Prepare Niuxi; fried and peeled Haritaki, 1 liang; processed Aconite; Angelica, each 1 liang; dried ginger; Chuanxiong, each 0.5 liang; Cinnamon heart; Baishao; Baizhu; Qianghuo, each 0.3 liang; Magnolia bark, peeled away from the coarse skin and roasted with fresh ginger juice until fragrant, 1.5 liang.
Grind these into a fine powder, mix with wine to form a paste, and knead into balls about the size of a phoenix seed. For each dose, take 30 pills, washed down with warm wine before meals.[69p]

Bichai Wine: Treats five types of lower back pain, including tightness and soreness in the leg and knee tendons.
Ingredients: Bichai and Niuxi, each three taels; Qianghuo, Fuzi (processed, skin and navel removed), each two taels; Dog spine, Duzhong (fried and de-fibred), each two taels; Gui Xin, Sang Jisheng, each two taels.
Method: Finely grind the above, place in a silk bag, soak in two dou of wine, seal tightly for seven days, then open. Take one cup, warmed, before meals.

Chenxiang Pills: Treats cold stagnation due to kidney deficiency, chronic lower back pain, numbness and pain in the legs and knees, weakness, and emaciation.
Ingredients: Chenxiang, Gui Xin, Bichai, Huai Gandi Huang, Niuxi, Qianghuo, Bai Fuling, Hai Tong Pi, Duzhong (peeled and roasted until yellow), Shihua (roots removed), Binglang, and Loulu, each three fen; Xiongfu, Mukang, and Danggui (lightly fried), Bai Zhu, and Fangfeng, each half a tael; Fuzi (peeled and processed), and Buguzhi (lightly fried), each one tael.
Method: Grind into a fine powder, knead with honey, and pound with a pestle for three to four thousand times. Form into pills the size of a phoenix seed. Take thirty pills on an empty stomach with warm wine, and take again in the evening as before.

Chaihu Decoction: Treats lower back pain with excess heat symptoms.
Ingredients: Chaihu, two to three qian; Huangqin, Shengdi, Chenpi, each one and a half qian; Shaoyao, two qian; Gan Cao, eight fen.
Method: Boil in one mug of water until reduced to seven or eight parts; drink warm.[70p]

Zheng Chai Hu Decoction: It treats lower back pain due to exterior wind-cold, suitable for balanced blood and qi, and is meant for gentle dispersal. Dang Gui Di Huang Decoction: It treats lower back and knee pain due to kidney deficiency. Zuo Gui Pill: It treats lower back pain due to kidney deficiency, specifically for true yin deficiency, strengthening water to nourish the left kidney's original yin, thus replenishing essence and blood. Ingredients: cooked rehmannia 8 liang; stir-fried Chinese yam, goji berries, cornelian cherry fruit, prepared dodder seeds, deer gelatin (stir-fried), tortoise shell gelatin (stir-fried), each 4 liang; for non-fires, do not use. For the achyranthes, wash and steam it with wine until cooked, 3 liang; for smoothness, don’t use. Next, steam the cooked rehmannia until soft and grind into a paste, mix with honey, and form into pills the size of tung seeds. Take with boiling soup or lightly salted soup before meals, about a hundred pills.[71p]

Right Return Pill: Treats kidney deficiency with腰痛, insufficient true yin, benefits the source of fire, nurturing the original yang of the right kidney, thus strengthening the spirit and energy. Ingredients include: Eight taels of cooked rehmannia, four taels each of lightly fried yam, lightly fried cornelian cherry flesh, lightly fried goji berries, fried deer horn glue, processed dodder seed, and fried eucommia in ginger juice; three taels of angelica, which should not be used if loose; two taels of cinnamon, which can gradually be increased to four taels; two taels of processed aconite, which can gradually be increased to five or six taels. Preparation for medicinal use:

  1. For the decoction, take ten taels of raw Rehmannia, along with one tael each of Achyranthes bidentata, Notopterygium incisum, Lycium barbarum bark, Acanthopanax bark, Chuanxiong (Szechuan lovage), Job's tears, and liquorice. Add two taels of sea mulberry bark. Grind them together and wrap in silk, then soak in two dou of good wine for 27 days, or alternatively for five days in summer. Take one cup each time, three to four times a day, ensuring the aroma of the wine remains potent. One variation includes one tael of Eucommia bark, fried until broken.

  2. Sheng Fu Decoction: Used for treating damp-related lower back pain.
    Ingredients: Raw Aconite, White atractylodes, Poria, Achyranthes bidentata, Magnolia officinalis, Dry ginger, and roasted liquorice, each one qian (a small unit). Additionally, two qian each of fried Cangzhu (Atractylodes), and Eucommia bark. Prepare one dose with two sheng of water, three slices of ginger, and two red dates, and boil until reduced to one sheng. Take before meals.

  3. Tangerine Seed Wine: Treats trauma-related lower back pain, stagnant blood accumulation, and severe pain. Roast tangerine seeds, remove the skin, and grind finely. Take two qian each time, mix with wine, or use one pig's kidney, removing membranes, breaking it apart with scallions, fennel, and salt, then wrap in wet paper and steam until cooked. Chew finely, and take with warm wine.

  4. Chuanxiong and Cinnamon Decoction: Treats lower back pain due to cold and dampness, accompanied by acute pain in the sides.
    Ingredients: Notopterygium, Bupleurum, Angelica sinensis stems, roasted liquorice, Chuanxiong (Szechuan lovage), cinnamon, and Cangzhu, each one qian; three fen each of Fangfeng (Siler) and Han Fangji. Additionally, five fen each of fried Quli (fermented grain) and Du Huo (angelica), and five peach kernels with skins removed, ground into a paste. Prepare as a decoction with wine, strain, and take warm far from meals.[74p]

　　麻黄苍朮汤 【《奇效良方》】 　治寒湿所客，身体沉重，腰痛，面色萎黄不泽。　　麻黄　泽泻　炒曲　白茯苓　橘皮各一钱　半夏　桂枝　草豆蔻　猪苓各半钱　苍朮　甘草炙各二钱黄芪三钱　杏仁十个　　右作一服，水二锺，煎一锺，食前服。

Grind into a fine powder, take 0.1 liang each time, dissolve in black bean wine to consume. The medicinal vapors will soon relieve the pain.

Mi Rong Wan
Treats kidney deficiency and腰痛, unable to turn side.
Deer antler and reindeer antler available.
One or two taels of Cuscuta seeds powder, half a tael of Fructus Foeniculi,
Grind the above into powder, use two pairs of sheep kidneys, soak in wine and cook until soft, remove the membrane and mash into a paste, form into pills the size of tung nuts, dry in the shade. If there are fewer sheep kidneys, add in some wine to paste and take 30 to 50 pills with warm wine or salted water.

Suan Zao Ren (skin removed, fried), each in equal parts, with Licorice cut in half.
Grind the above into powder, add pig spine marrow mixed with Dihuang paste to form pills.

　　杜仲　肉苁蓉　破故纸　人参　当归　秋石　川巴戟　鹿角霜各等分　　右为末，用猪腰子一个，洗净血水，淡盐浥过，劈开两半，勿令断，中间细华开，用前药掺入，另用稀绢一块包裹，线缚定，外用小糖罐，入酒少许，罐上用纸封固，毋令走泄药气，煮腰子候熟取食之，饮醇酒三五杯，立愈。
　　立安丸　治五种腰痛，常服补暖肾经，壮健腰脚。　　破故纸　干木瓜　杜仲去皮，姜炒去丝　续断　牛膝酒浸，各一两　萆薢二两　　右为细末，炼蜜丸如梧桐子大，每服五十丸，空心用温酒或盐汤送下。
　　二至丸　治肾气虚损，腰痛，不可屈伸。　　附子炮去皮脐　桂心　杜仲去皮，銼，炒去丝　补骨脂炒，各一两　鹿角镑　麋角镑，各二两　鹿茸酒炙　青盐另研，各半两　　右为细末，酒煮糊和丸如梧桐子大，每服七十丸，空心用胡桃肉细嚼，用盐汤或盐酒送下。如恶热药者，去附子加肉苁蓉一两。
　　速效散　治男女腰痛不可忍者。[81p]

Du Zhong, Rou Cong Rong, Po Gu Zhi, Ren Shen, Dang Gui, Qiu Shi, Chuan Ba Ji, Lu Jiao Shuang, each in equal parts.

Grind them into a fine powder. Take one pig kidney, clean it of blood, rinse with light salt water, cut it in half without breaking it, and make a small slit in the middle. Mix in the powdered herbs, wrap it in a thin silk cloth, tie it securely with string, place it in a small sugar jar, add a little wine, seal the jar tightly with paper to prevent the medicinal vapors from escaping. Cook the kidney until done, take it out and eat, then drink three to five cups of fine wine for immediate recovery.

Li An Wan treats five types of lower back pain; taking it regularly warms the kidney channels and strengthens the waist and legs.

Po Gu Zhi, dried papaya, Du Zhong (de-skinned), ginger (stir-fried and stringy removed), Xu Dui (a type of Chinese herb), Niu Xi (wine-soaked), each one liang; Bai Xi (two liang).

Grind into a fine powder, then refine with honey into pills the size of the seeds of a phoenix tree. Take fifty pills each time, on an empty stomach with warm wine or salt water.

Er Zhi Wan treats renal qi deficiency and related back pain, preventing bending and stretching.

Fu Zi (peeled and prepared), Gui Xin, Du Zhong (de-skinned, shredded, stir-fried), Bu Gu Zhi (stir-fried), each one liang; Lu Jiao Bang, Mi Jiao Bang, each two liang; Lu Rong (wine-dried), Qing Yan (separately ground), each half a liang.

Grind into a fine powder, boil with wine until thick, then form pills the size of the seeds of a phoenix tree. Take seventy pills each time, on an empty stomach, chewing them with walnut meat, and wash down with saltwater or salted wine. If one reacts poorly to the heat of the medicine, omit Fu Zi and add one liang of Rou Cong Rong instead.

Su Xiao San treats unbearable back pain in both men and women.[81p]

　　川楝子取肉，以巴豆五粒去壳，同炒赤，去巴豆　茴香盐炒香，去盐　破故纸炒，各一两　　右为细末，每服三钱，空心热酒调服。
　　散滞丸　治腰痛不可忍者。
　　黑牵牛不以多少，取头末
　　右用大蒜，每一瓣入巴豆肉一粒在内，以湿纸裹定，煨香熟，去巴豆，将蒜研和牵牛末为丸梧子大，每服五丸，空心食前酢茶汤下，量虚实服。一方无巴豆，以朱砂为衣，每服二十丸酒下，一服便安。　　又方　治腰痛。
　　胡桃肉　补骨脂　杜仲各四两
　　右(口父)咀，作二贴，每贴用水二盏煎，空心服。
　　张走马家飞步丸　此第一方筋骨药，能去筋脉骨节手足腰背诸般疼痛，挛缩不伸之患。　　乳香一两，另研　白芍药　川乌生，刮去皮脐　草乌生，刮去皮脐　木鳖子取肉，另研去油净　白胶香各二两　　右为细末，用赤小豆末煮糊为丸如梧子大，每服十五丸，木瓜汤下。病在上，食后服；病在下，空心服。忌热物片时。[82p]

Chuanlianzi (fruit of the neem tree) is taken for its flesh. With five 巴豆 (castor beans) shelled, stir-fry until red and remove the 巴豆. Stir-fry with fennel and salt until fragrant, then remove the salt. Break old paper and stir-fry, with each ingredient measuring one tael. Grind them into fine powder, and take three qian (a unit of weight) each time, mixed with hot wine on an empty stomach. This is a remedy for waist pain that is unbearable.

For another remedy, take the black morning glory, regardless of the quantity, and grind its head into powder. Use garlic; each clove should contain one piece of 巴豆 flesh, wrap in damp paper, and cook until fragrant and done. Remove the 巴豆, mash the garlic with the morning glory powder into pills the size of walnuts. Take five pills before meals with vinegar tea; adjust the dosage based on the condition. If there is no 巴豆, use vermilion as a coating, taking twenty pills with wine, which will provide immediate relief.

Another formula for treating waist pain includes four taels each of walnut meat, bu guo zi (Psoralea fruit), and du zhong (eucommia). These should be chewed and made into two plasters. Each plaster is boiled with two bowls of water and taken on an empty stomach.

Zhang Zouma's Feibu Pills are the primary formula for muscle and bone ailments, effective for relieving pains and stiffness in tendons, bones, waist, back, and other painful conditions. Ingredients include one tael of frankincense, ground separately, along with white peony root, whole Chuanwu (prepared), whole Cao Wu (prepared), and the flesh of wood navel fruit (also ground and cleaned of oil), each two taels. Grind these into fine powder and make pills the size of walnuts using red adzuki bean paste to bind. Take fifteen pills with papaya soup; if the condition is on top, take after meals; if on the bottom, take on an empty stomach. Avoid heating foods temporarily.[82p]

Shen Ying Pill: Treats insufficiency of the kidney meridian, with wind and cold affecting it, causing back pain as if broken, pulling at the back when bending or standing. This could be due to overwork injuring the kidneys, lying on damp ground, falling and sustaining injuries, or being attacked by cold wind, all leading to back pain.
Ingredients: 2 taels each of Wei Ling Xian, Gui Xin, and Dang Gui.
Grind these into a fine powder, mix with wine to form pills the size of walnuts. Take 20-30 pills before meals with warm wine or fennel soup. For women, take with Gui Xin soup.

Ru Shen Decoction: Also known as Shu Jin Decoction or Li Xiao Powder. Treats back pain in both men and women, with stagnation of blood and abdominal pain, especially effective post childbirth.
Ingredients: Equal parts of Yan Hu Suo (slightly toasted), Dang Gui, and Gui Xin.
Grind into a fine powder, take 2 qian at any time, adjusted with warm wine. Another variation may add Du Zhong, or also include Tao Ren (peach kernels), Niu Xi (ox knee), and Xu Duan (Chinese teasel).

Qian Niu Pill: Treats cold air flow blocking, with back pain making it impossible to bend or stand.
Ingredients: 2 taels each of Hei Qian Niu (black morning glory), Yan Hu Suo (toasted), and Bu Gu Zhi (additional toasted).
Grind these, prepare garlic paste, and form into pills the size of walnuts. Take 50 pills before meals with onion wine and salt soup. In one variation, omit Yan Hu Suo and use Bu Gu Zhi ground with wheat flour to make pills with wine.

Li An Powder: Specifically treats back pain.
Ingredients: Equal parts of toasted Du Zhong and toasted tangerine seeds, using the kernels.
Grind into a fine powder, take 2 qian at any time, adjusted with salt wine.[83p]

Bu Gu Zhi Wan treats unbearable lower back pain.
Two liang of Bu Gu Zhi, soaked in wine overnight, stir-fried with bran until done. Apricot seeds, peeled and ground, and peach kernels, peeled and ground, each one liang. An Wan treats sudden falling or twisting injuries, blood and qi stagnation, and lower back pain.
An Zi, soaked in wine and baked; Wei Ling Xian, roasted and crushed; Du Zhong, stir-fried with ginger juice to remove fibers; Gui Xin, each five qian; Myrrh and Frankincense, each two and a half qian, separately ground. All ingredients are ground into fine powder, boiled with wine and flour to form pills the size of a giant ginkgo nut. Each dose is seventy pills, taken with warm salt water or salt wine as desired.

Shen Qu Jiu treats injuries and strains of lower back pain.
One piece of Shen Qu, about the size of a fist, burn until red. Mix with two large cups of good wine and drink it all at once. Lie on your back for a little while, and you will feel at ease. Alternatively, taking Qing E Wan with this wine is particularly effective.

Chu Shi Dan treats lower back pain due to kidney issues.
Four liang of dried tangerine peel, two liang each of betel nut, Euphorbia, cooked peony root, Wei Ling Xian, Phragmipedium, and Tian Ma; one liang each of crushed black morning glory seeds, Myrrh, and Frankincense, all separately ground; three liang of stir-fried Euphorbia. Grind all into powder, mix with flour to form pills the size of a giant ginkgo nut. Each dose is thirty-nine pills, taken with warm lampwick tea.[84p]

Zhuangben Dan: Treats kidney deficiency and severe lower back pain very effectively.

Prepare wine-fried Du Zhong, stir-fried Pó Gù Zhǐ, and stir-fried Fennel, each one liang; wash with wine the meat of Cóng Róng, soak Ba Jí in wine; use five qian each of salt. Grind these into a powder. Split pig kidneys, insert the medicine inside, sew them shut, wrap in paper, and steam until cooked. Each one constitutes a dose, to be taken with yellow wine.

Ju Fang An Shen Wan: Treats kidney deficiency, lower back pain, coldness in the lower source, and frequent and slippery urination. Ingredients include: Tao Ren, Bai Ji Li, Ba Jí, Ròu Cóng Róng, Shan Yao, Shí Hú, Pó Gù Zhǐ, Bai Fú Líng, Bǐ Xiè, Bai Zhū each 2 liang 4 qian; Chuan Wǔ Pào and Ròu Guì each 1 liang 3 qian. Bu Sui Dan: Treats kidney deficiency and lower back pain. 　　右同炒令焦黄色，以水一盏浸一宿，五更去滓服，天明取下如鸡肝者，即恶物也。

Cooked Rhubarb Decoction
For treating falls, sprains, and腰 pain that prevents bending or stretching.
Ingredients:

  • Cut rhubarb to the size of a finger
  • Ginger – each 0.5 taels
    Sauté until brown, soak in one cup of water overnight. Drink after removing dregs at dawn; if the concoction resembles chicken liver in the morning, it is harmful.

For treating kidney deficiency and lower back pain.

Grind these into a powder; take one qian with salt water, at any time.

Blood Breaking Pain Relief Soup (from "The Ten Books of Dongyuan")
For treating injuries from a fall, specifically affecting the lower back; stasis blood beneath the ribs causing pain that prevents movement.
Three qian of leech, fried until smoke dissipates, then ground finely; two qian each of Lianqiao, Danggui, and Chaihu; one and a half qian of Sumu; one qian each of Qianghuo, Fangfeng, and Gui Xin; half a qian of musk, ground separately.
Grind and divide into two doses; take with two cups of wine and one cup of water, simmer until one cup remains, remove dregs, mix in leech and musk powder, and take on an empty stomach; two doses will lead to recovery.

Channel Unblocking Powder (from "Confucianism and Parental Guidance")
For treating lower back pain caused by dampness from water.
Equal parts of Chenpi, Danggui, and Gansui.
Grind into a powder; take three qian, mixed with warm wine before bedtime.[88p]

Shengjindan: For treating lower back sores and all types of swellings and pains.[89p]

　　麝香　制砒各五分　蟾酥一钱　雄黄　辰砂　乳香　没药　血竭各一钱半　天龙去头足，炙　全蝎泡，炙　穿山甲炙，各三钱　僵蚕炙去丝，五钱　　右为细末，和匀，每服三分，赤砂糖调葱头酒送下，取汗为度。
　　内疏黄连汤　治缠腰火丹，并一切痈疽，发热而烦，脉沉而实，病远在内，脏腑秘濇，当急疏利之。　　连翘二两　黄连　芍药　当归　槟榔　木香　黄牛　栀子　薄荷　桔梗　甘草各一两　　右除槟榔、木香为末外，并銼，每服一两，水一盏半，煎一盏，先吃一二服，次每服加大黄一钱，再加二钱，以利为度。
　　一粒金丹　治一切恶疮痈肿，无名肿毒。　　沉香　木香　乳香各五分　巴豆霜一钱五分　　右为细末，照称分数和匀，用黑肥枣子个半去皮捣烂为丸，如芡实大，每服一丸。量人虚实，先呷水一口，行一次。胃气壮实者，只可呷水三四口，不可太过，后用水一口送药下，行尽数次，以米饮补之。[90p]

Musk, arsenic each five fen, toad venom one qian, realgar, cinnabar, frankincense, myrrh, and dragon's blood each one and a half qian. Remove the head and feet of the sky dragon, and roast. Soak whole scorpions, and roast; roast pangolins, each three qian. Silkworms, roasted and stripped of silk, five qian. The right side is finely powdered and mixed well. Take three fen each time, adjust with red sand sugar and scallion wine to swallow, depending on the individual's sweating.

The "Inner Dismissal of Huanglian Decoction" treats the fiery accumulation of the waist, as well as all festering sores and abscesses, characterized by heat and agitation, with a deep and firm pulse, indicating that the illness is within, and the organs are secretly obstructed; immediate expulsion is necessary.

Two liang of forsythia, yellow lantern, peony, angelica, betel nut, wood fragrance, yellow cow, gardenia, mint, platycodon, and licorice, each one liang. The right side, except for betel nut and wood fragrance, should be powdered and ground fine; each dose is one liang, with one and a half cups of water, decocted to one cup. First take one or two doses, then for each subsequent dose, add one qian of rhubarb, and increase by two qian, adjusting for laxation.

A single golden pill treats all evil sores, abscesses, and unnamed swellings. Five fen each of fragrant wood, wood fragrance, and frankincense, and one and a half qian of purgative bean powder. The right side is finely powdered, mixed according to ranks, and formed into pills with half a black fat jujube, peeled and mashed to the size of a water chestnut. Take one pill each time. According to one's level of deficiency or excess, sip a mouthful of water, and engage in a single action. Those with robust stomach Qi may only sip three or four mouthfuls, without excessive intake. Afterward, use a mouthful of water to swallow the medicine, and repeat several times, supplementing with rice drink.[90p]

　　仙方活命饮　一名真人活命饮。治一切疮疡，未成脓者内消，已成脓者即溃，又止痛消毒之圣药也。　　滴乳香研　当归尾　明没药研　赤芍　防风　甘草节　白芷　贝母　皂角刺炒　天花粉　穿山甲炮，各一钱　陈皮　金银花各三钱　　右为粗末，大者四者、小者二两作一剂，无灰洒十茶锺，疮小五茶锺，入有嘴瓶内，以厚纸封口，勿令泄气，煎至三大锺，去滓，作三次服，接连不断，随疮上下服。能饮酒者，服药后再饮三五杯。此药并无酒气，不动脏腑，不伤气血。忌酸、薄酒、铁器，服后侧睡，觉痛定回生，神功浩大，不可臆度。
　　人参养荣汤　治痈疽气血不足，不能收敛，若大疮愈后，多服之不变他病。　　白芍一钱半　人参　陈皮　黄芪蜜炙　桂心　当归酒拌　白朮　甘草炙，各一钱　熟地酒拌　五味炒杵　茯苓各七分半　远志去心炒，五分　　右作一剂，水二锺，姜三片，枣一枚，煎八分，食前服。[91p]

Immortal Life Potion — also known as the True Person's Life Potion. It treats all types of sores and ulcers; those that have not yet turned to pus are resolved internally, and those that have turned to pus will break open. It is a sacred remedy that also alleviates pain and disinfects.

Ingredients:

  • Frankincense powder
  • Angelica tail
  • Myrrh powder
  • Red peony
  • Siler root
  • Licorice stems
  • White atractylodes
  • Fritillaria
  • Saponaria pods, roasted
  • Trichosanthes root
  • Ground pangolin shell, each one qian (a unit of weight)
  • Dried tangerine peel
  • Honeysuckle, three qian each.

Mix these into a coarse powder. For larger sores use four qian of the larger ingredients and two liang of the smaller ones to make one dose. Add ten tea bowls of water for larger sores or five tea bowls for smaller ones. Place in a bottle with a mouth, sealing it tightly with thick paper to prevent air leakage. Boil down to three bowls, remove the residue, and take this three times without interruption, adjusting the dosage according to the condition of the sores. Those who can drink alcohol may consume three to five cups after taking the medicine. This potion does not carry the taste of alcohol, does not disturb the internal organs, and does not harm qi and blood. Avoid sour foods, thin alcohol, and iron utensils; sleep on one's side after taking it. Pain relief may be swift and revitalizing, exhibiting remarkable efficacy that cannot be underestimated.

Ginseng Nourishing Decoction — used to treat boils and carbuncles caused by deficiency of qi and blood, which prevents healing. If a large sore has healed, taking this remedy regularly will not lead to other illnesses.

Ingredients:

  • White peony, one and a half qian
  • Ginseng
  • Dried tangerine peel
  • Honey-fried Astragalus
  • Cinnamon bark
  • Wine-soaked Angelica
  • Atractylodes
  • Honey-fried licorice, each one qian
  • Wine-soaked cooked Rehmannia
  • Stir-fried Schisandra berries, seven and a half fen each
  • Stir-fried Polygala root, five fen.

Prepare as one dose, adding two bowls of water, three slices of ginger, and one jujube. Boil down to eight parts and consume before meals.[91p]

　　十全大补汤　治血气未足之人，结肿未成脓者，宜加枳壳、香附、连翘，服之自消。　　人参　肉桂　地黄酒洗，蒸焙　白芍炒　川芎　白茯苓　白朮黄土水拌炒　黄芪盐水拌炒　当归酒拌，各一钱　甘草炙，五分　　右作一剂，用水二锺，姜枣煎服。

腰门

　　　　单方
　　金牙石：治一切冷风气筋骨挛急，腰脚不遂，烧酒浸服。 【甄权】
　　脾疼腰痛：砒霜成块者为末，黄丹各半两，化蜡入砒，以柳条搅，焦则换，至七条取起收之，每旋丸梧子大，冷水送下。小儿黍米大。【《和剂局方》】
　　腰腹诸痛：焰硝、雄黄各一钱，研细末，每点少许入眦内，名火龙丹。 【《集元方》】
　　腰脚疼痛：天麻、半夏、细辛各二两，绢袋二个各盛药，合匀蒸热，交互熨痛处，汗出则愈，数日再熨。【《卫生易简方》】
　　气滞腰痛：青木香、乳香各二钱，酒浸饭上蒸匀，酒调服。 【《圣惠方》】[92p]

Complete Nourishing Decoction

For individuals with insufficient blood and qi, and when lumps have not yet formed pus, add bitter orange peel, cyperus, and forsythia. Taking these will help dissolve them.

Ingredients:

  • Ginseng
  • Cassia
  • Wine-washed and steamed Rehmannia
  • Fried white peony
  • Chuanxiong
  • White poria
  • White atractylodes mixed with yellow earth and stir-fried
  • Astragalus stir-fried in salt water
  • Angelica mixed with wine, each 1 qian (3 grams)
  • Honey-fried licorice, 0.5 qian (1.5 grams)

Use these as one dose, boil with two sheng (about 500 ml) of water, add ginger and jujubes, and decoct for consumption.

Waist and Lower Back Treatments

Single Formulas:

  • Jin Yashi: Treats all sorts of cold wind causing contractions in the muscles and bones, resulting in an inability to move the waist and legs. Soak and consume with strong liquor. [Zhen Quan]

  • Spleen and Waist Pain: Use arsenic in chunks, half a liang (15 grams) of yellow lead each, mix with wax by stirring with willow twigs. When charred, replace it, and collect seven twigs; each should be formed into pills the size of a wutong nut, swallowed with cold water. For children, use the size of millet grains. [From "He Ji Ju Fang"]

  • Waist and Abdominal Pain: Use gunpowder and realgar, each 1 qian (3 grams), grind into fine powder, and apply a small amount to the inner corners of the eyes, known as Fire Dragon Pill. [From "Ji Yuan Fang"]

  • Waist and Leg Pain: Use tianma (Gastrodia elata), banxia (Pinellia), and xixin (Asarum), each 2 liang (60 grams). Place the medicine into two silk bags, steam and heat them, then alternately apply to the painful spots. Sweating will lead to recovery; repeat for several days. [From "Weisheng Yi Jian Fang"]

  • Qi Stagnation Causing Waist Pain: Use Qingmuxiang (a type of aromatic herb) and frankincense, each 2 qian (6 grams), soak in liquor, steam with rice and consume with liquor. [From "Sheng Hui Fang"][92p]

　　肾虚腰痛：用破故纸一两炒为末，温酒服三钱，神妙；或加木香一钱。 【《经验方》】
　　腰痛：揩牙香附子五两，生姜二两，取自然汁浸一宿，炒黄为末，入青盐二钱，擦牙数次，其痛即止。【《乾坤生意》】
　　妇人腰痛：向东蘘荷根一把，捣汁三升服之。 【《肘后方》】
　　腰脚风气作痛：大黄一两，切如棋子，和少酥炒干，勿令焦，捣筛，每用二钱，空心以水三大合，入姜三片，煎十余沸，取汤调服，当下冷脓恶物，痛即止。【崔元亮《海上方》】
　　腰脚冷痹疼痛有风：川乌头三个，生，去皮脐为散，酢调涂帛上，贴之，须臾痛止。 【《圣惠方》】
　　虚寒腰痛：鹿茸去毛，酥炙微黄，附子炮去皮脐各二两，盐花三分为末，枣肉和丸，梧子大，每服三十丸，空心温酒下。
　　腰膝疼痛，或顽麻无力：菟丝子洗一两，牛膝一两，同入银器内，酒浸一寸五分，暴为末，将原酒煮糊，丸梧子大，每空心酒服二三十丸。【《经验方》】[93p]

Kidney deficiency and lower back pain: Use one tael of broken old paper, fry it to a powder, and take three qian with warm wine; it's miraculous; or add one qian of wood fragrance.

Lower back pain: Grind five liang of clove and two liang of fresh ginger, soak in natural juice overnight, fry until yellow into a powder, add two qian of green salt, rub on the teeth several times, and the pain will stop.

Lower back pain in women: Take a handful of Dongxianghong root, pound it to extract three sheng of juice and take it.

Wind pain in lower back and legs: One tael of rhubarb, cut into chess piece size, mix with a little oil and fry dry without burning, pound and sift; use two qian with water three large bowls, add three slices of ginger, boil for over ten bubbles, take the soup as needed to eliminate cold pus and pains will stop.

Cold blockage and pain in lower back and legs due to wind: Three pieces of Chuanwu root, raw, peel and remove the navel, scatter and mix with vinegar, apply on cloth and stick it; the pain will stop shortly.

Deficiency cold lower back pain: Deer antler, remove fur, slightly fried until yellow; two liang each of Aconite root (processed without skin) and salt flower ground to powder, mix with jujube flesh to form pills the size of a walnut, take thirty pills with warm wine on an empty stomach.

Lower back and knee pain, or stubborn numbness and weakness: One liang of Cuscuta seed, one liang of牛膝 (Niu Xi), both placed in silver container, soak in wine for one and a half inches, pound to powder, cook the original wine until thick, make pills the size of a walnut, take twenty to thirty pills with wine on an empty stomach.[93p]

　　气滞腰痛：牵牛不拘多少，以新瓦烧赤安于上，自然一半生，一半熟，不得拨动，取末一两，入硫黄未二钱半，同研匀，分作三分，每分用白面三匙，水和捍开，切作棋子。五更初以水一盏煮熟，连汤温下，痛即已。未住，隔日再作。予常有此疾，每发一服，痛即止。【《本事方》】
　　挫气腰痛：香茶内滴入菜油数点，顿服。 【《纲目》】
　　腰重作痛：槟榔为末，酒服一钱。 【《斗门方》】
　　桄榔子，面作饼，炙食，腴美令人不饥，补益虚羸损乏，腰脚无力，久服轻身辟谷。 【李珣】
　　腰痛难转：煎茶五合，投酢二合，顿服。 【孟诜《食疗》】
　　腰腿疼痛：甜瓜子三两，酒浸十日为末，每服三钱，空心酒下，日三。 【《寿域神方》】
　　闪挫腰痛：用西瓜青皮，阴干为末，盐酒调服三钱。 【《摄生众妙方》】[94p]

Qi stagnation leading to lower back pain: Use an unbound quantity of morning glory, burn it using new tiles until it turns red and place it above. Naturally, it will contain both raw and cooked elements. Do not stir it. Take one or two taels of the powder, mix it with two and a half qian of sulfur, grind it evenly, and divide it into three parts. For each part, use three spoonfuls of white flour, mix with water, and shape it like chess pieces. Boil one cup of water in the early morning until cooked, and drink the warm broth; the pain will cease. If the pain persists, repeat the process the next day. I often have this ailment, and upon taking one dose, the pain immediately stops.

Bruised qi leading to back pain: Add a few drops of vegetable oil into fragrant tea and take it all at once.
